<td>URTEXT-Richard Johnson Editions of Clara Schumann's authoritative edition of the works of her husband Robert Schumann published by Breitkopf &amp; Härtel, researched and updated according to recent urtext editions. All works feature complete fingerings and very readable musical text. See title page of individual works for more information.

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Kinderszenen
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Leichte Stücke
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Schumann,_Robert" title="Category:Schumann, Robert">Schumann, Robert</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.15
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IRS 69
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>13 pieces:
<ol><li> Von fremden Ländern und Menschen (G major)<br /><small>(Of Foreign Lands and Peoples / Des pays mystérieux)</small>
</li><li> Kuriose Geschichte (D major)<br /><small>(A Curious Story / Histoire curieuse)</small>
</li><li> Hasche-Mann (B minor)<br /><small>(Blind Man's Buff / Colin-Maillard)</small>
</li><li> Bittendes Kind (D major)<br /><small>(Pleading Child / L'enfant qui prie)</small>
</li><li> Glückes genug (D major)<br /><small>(Happy Enough / Bonheur parfait)</small>
</li><li> Wichtige Begebenheit (A major)<br /><small>(An Important Event / Grande nouvelle)</small>
</li><li> Träumerei (F major)<br /><small>(Dreaming / Rêverie)</small>
</li><li> Am Kamin (F major)<br /><small>(At The Fireside / Au coin du feu)</small>, F major
</li><li> Ritter vom Steckenpferd (C major)<br /><small>(Knight Of The Hobbyhorse / Sur le cheval de bois)</small>
</li><li> Fast zu ernst (G-sharp minor}<br /><small>(Almost Too Serious / Peut-être trop sérieux)</small>
</li><li> Fürchtenmachen (E minor)<br /><small>(Frightening / Faire peur)</small>
</li><li> Kind im Einschlummern (E minor)<br /><small>(Child Falling Asleep / L'enfant s'endort)</small>
</li><li> Der Dichter spricht (G major)<br /><small>(The Poet Speaks / Le poète parle)</small>
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1838
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1839 – Leipzig: <a href="/wiki/Breitkopf_und_H%C3%A4rtel" title="Breitkopf und Härtel">Breitkopf und Härtel</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
